<span data-ttu-id="04cad-849">Cette classe contient les attributs suivants pour Windows Server 2003 R2 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="04cad-849">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2003 R2:</span></span>
